     <div class="uk-container uk-container-center">
      <article class="uk-article">
       <h1 class="l-section-intro--title uk-article-title">
        Welcome to Colorado’s Flagship Christian University
       </h1>
       <div class="uk-grid uk-visible-large">
        <div class="uk-width-1-4">
         <figure class="uk-overlay image-overlay is-disabled">
          <a class="" href="/undergrad/" target="_self">
          </a>
          <img alt="" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/dg5ir1kvd/image/fetch/fl_advanced_resize%2Cc_thumb%2Cw_226%2Ch_198/https://www.ccu.edu/_files/images/students-walking-down-pathway.jpg%3Fv%3D1532844059030"/>
          <figcaption class="uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-bottom image-overlay--overlay">
           <div class="image-overlay--visible uk-vertical-align">
            <span class="image-overlay--title uk-vertical-align-middle">
             Undergraduate Majors
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="image-overlay--hidden">
            <p class="uk-animation-fade">
             The College of Undergraduate Studies offers over 50 programs for traditional students.
            </p>
            <footer class="image-overlay--footer uk-animation-fade">
             Read More
            </footer>
           </div>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
        </div>
        <div class="uk-width-1-4">
         <figure class="uk-overlay image-overlay is-disabled">
          <a class="" href="/ccu/programs/" target="_self">
          </a>
          <img alt="" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/dg5ir1kvd/image/fetch/fl_advanced_resize%2Cc_thumb%2Cw_226%2Ch_198/https://www.ccu.edu/_files/images/colorado%20christian%20university/adult-students-in-class.jpg%3Fv%3D1532844059030"/>
          <figcaption class="uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-bottom image-overlay--overlay">
           <div class="image-overlay--visible uk-vertical-align">
            <span class="image-overlay--title uk-vertical-align-middle">
             Adult Degree Programs
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="image-overlay--hidden">
            <p class="uk-animation-fade">
             Adult students can complete their associate or bachelor’s degree or earn a certificate.
            </p>
            <footer class="image-overlay--footer uk-animation-fade">
             Read More
            </footer>
           </div>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
        </div>
        <div class="uk-width-1-4">
         <figure class="uk-overlay image-overlay is-disabled">
          <a class="" href="/ccu/grad/" target="_self">
          </a>
          <img alt="" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/dg5ir1kvd/image/fetch/fl_advanced_resize%2Cc_thumb%2Cw_226%2Ch_198/https://www.ccu.edu/_files/images/colorado%20christian%20university/business-people-working.jpg%3Fv%3D1532844059030"/>
          <figcaption class="uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-bottom image-overlay--overlay">
           <div class="image-overlay--visible uk-vertical-align">
            <span class="image-overlay--title uk-vertical-align-middle">
             Graduate Degree Programs
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="image-overlay--hidden">
            <p class="uk-animation-fade">
             Take your career to a new level with a master’s degree from CCU.
            </p>
            <footer class="image-overlay--footer uk-animation-fade">
             Read More
            </footer>
           </div>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
        </div>
        <div class="uk-width-1-4">
         <figure class="uk-overlay image-overlay is-disabled">
          <a class="" href="/ccu/online/" target="_self">
          </a>
          <img alt="" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/dg5ir1kvd/image/fetch/fl_advanced_resize%2Cc_thumb%2Cw_226%2Ch_198/https://www.ccu.edu/_files/images/colorado%20christian%20university/adult-student-learning-on-computer.jpg%3Fv%3D1532844059030"/>
          <figcaption class="uk-overlay-panel uk-overlay-bottom image-overlay--overlay">
           <div class="image-overlay--visible uk-vertical-align">
            <span class="image-overlay--title uk-vertical-align-middle">
             Online Programs + Degrees
            </span>
           </div>
           <div class="image-overlay--hidden">
            <p class="uk-animation-fade">
             CCU’s online degree programs let you earn a degree from home, the office, or on-the-go.
            </p>
            <footer class="image-overlay--footer uk-animation-fade">
             Read More
            </footer>
           </div>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p class="l-section-intro--content uk-article-lead">
       </p>
       <p>
        Colorado Christian University is located in Lakewood, Colorado, a suburb of Denver. Founded in 1914, CCU is the flagship Christian university in the Rocky Mountain region. A leader in higher education, the University is ranked in the
        <a href="/news/2016/ccu-ranked-in-top-two-percent-nationwide-five-years-in-a-row/">
         top two percent of colleges nationwide
        </a>
        for its core curriculum by the American Council of Trustees and Alumni. CCU is also noted as one of the “
        <a href="/news/2016/ccu-ranks-in-top-30-for-best-four-year-colleges-for-adult-learners/">
         Best Four-Year Colleges for Adult Learners"
        </a>
        by
        <em>
         Washington Monthly
        </em>
        .
       </p>
       <p>
        CCU offers more than 100 degree programs for traditional and adult students through its
        <a href="/undergrad/">
         College of Undergraduate Studies
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/ccu/">
         College of Adult and Graduate Studies
        </a>
        . More than 8,000 students attend the University on the main campus, in regional centers throughout Colorado and
        <a href="/ccu/online/">
         online
        </a>
        .
       </p>
       <div class="uk-grid uk-margin-large-top" data-uk-margin="{cls:'uk-margin-large-top'}">
        <div class="uk-width-medium-1-2 uk-flex uk-flex-center uk-flex-middle uk-container-center">
         <a href="/learnaboutsalvation/">
          <img alt="Who is Jesus" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/dg5ir1kvd/image/fetch/fl_advanced_resize%2Cc_limit%2Cw_735/https://www.ccu.edu/_files/images/icon-right-column/who-is-jesus.png%3Fv%3D1532844059030" title="Who is Jesus"/>
         </a>
        </div>
        <div class="uk-width-medium-1-2 uk-flex uk-flex-center uk-flex-middle uk-container-center">
         <a href="http://www.ccu.edu/centennial/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
          <img alt="Centennial Institute" src="https://res.cloudinary.com/dg5ir1kvd/image/fetch/fl_advanced_resize%2Cc_limit%2Cw_735/https://www.ccu.edu/_files/images/icon-right-column/ci-logo.png%3Fv%3D1532844059030" title="Centennial Institute"/>
         </a>
        </div>
       </div>
       <p>
       </p>
      </article>
     </div>
    </div>
   </section>
